SELECT [t].[Id], [t].[ApprovedBy], [t].[ApprovedOn], [t].[ContractNumber], [t].[ContractValue], [t].[CreatedOn], [t].[Description], [t].[EndDate], [t].[IsDeleted], [t].[IsRenewal], [t].[ParentContractId], [t].[RejectionReason], [t].[RenewalApprovedBy], [t].[RenewalApprovedOn], [t].[RenewalRequestedOn], [t].[StartDate], [t].[Status], [t].[SubmittedOn], [t].[TerminatedBy], [t].[TerminatedOn], [t].[TerminationReason], [t].[Title], [t].[UpdatedOn], [t].[VendorId], [v].[Id], [v].[Address], [v].[CompanyName], [v].[ContactPerson], [v].[CreatedOn], [v].[Email], [v].[GSTNumber], [v].[IsActive], [v].[IsDeleted], [v].[PANNumber], [v].[Phone], [v].[UpdatedOn], [v].[VendorName]
FROM (
    SELECT [c].[Id], [c].[ApprovedBy], [c].[ApprovedOn], [c].[ContractNumber], [c].[ContractValue], [c].[CreatedOn], [c].[Description], [c].[EndDate], [c].[IsDeleted], [c].[IsRenewal], [c].[ParentContractId], [c].[RejectionReason], [c].[RenewalApprovedBy], [c].[RenewalApprovedOn], [c].[RenewalRequestedOn], [c].[StartDate], [c].[Status], [c].[SubmittedOn], [c].[TerminatedBy], [c].[TerminatedOn], [c].[TerminationReason], [c].[Title], [c].[UpdatedOn], [c].[VendorId]
    FROM [Contracts] AS [c]
    WHERE [c].[IsDeleted] = CAST(0 AS bit)
    ORDER BY [c].[Id] DESC
    OFFSET @__p_0 ROWS FETCH NEXT @__p_1 ROWS ONLY
) AS [t]
INNER JOIN [Vendors] AS [v] ON [t].[VendorId] = [v].[Id]
ORDER BY [t].[Id] DESC
